* Dizziness: Ear pain often causes dizziness in the head.
* Hearing Ability: If this infection is ignored for a long time, the hearing power of the ear may be lost.

Treatments:
Treatment of Ear Infection
To avoid ear infection, it is important to take special care of cleanliness. Apart from this, ear infections can also be avoided by following some of the following things.
Cleaning of the wax - Excess wax in the ear causes ear infections by increasing bacteria in the ear. Ear waxes can be cleaned by physicians with microscopic instruments. Usually people clean the ear from the ear bud too, but if the wax is high then it cannot be cleaned with the ear bud.
Use of Ear Drops - Many times an ear medicine can also get rid of ear infections. Doctors give ear drops for ear pain, which removes wax along with ear pain.
Tips- (Prevent Ear Infection)
- In winter cold, eat and drink only after washing hands thoroughly.
- Avoid going out in the cold. The risk of infection is higher in crowded places.
- Avoid Smoking.

Home Remedies:
Home Remedies
1- If you have pain in the ear, grinding the marigold flower and adding its juice provides relief.
2- By heating salt and tying it in a cloth, compressing the ear also provides relief from ear pain.
3- Add garlic to the cooking oil and heat the oil. Put few drops of this oil in the ear three to four times.
4- Rubbing juice of basil leaves and rubbing it around the ear also provides relief. Take care not to put the juice inside the ear.
5- Add equal quantity of water in apple vinegar and soak cotton in it. Keep this cotton behind the ear for a while.
6- Heat the olive oil, put a few drops of lukewarm oil in your ear.
7- Enlarge the ears with a bottle of hot water.
8- Heat the onion and grind it in a grinder to extract the juice. Put a few drops of onion juice in your ear.


Disease: Diabetic Retinopathy

Description:
Diabetic retinopathy
Diabetic retinopathy is a disease that affects the retina (the curtain of the eye where the picture is made) of a person suffering from diabetes. This is due to the damage to the fine tubes that supply blood to the retina, if the person is not treated on time, the victim may become a victim of blindness. Diabetic retinopathy is the largest cause of blindness in the world, with cases increasing every year.

Symptoms:
- Repeated eye infection
- Change the number of glasses frequently
- Retina hemorrhage
- White cataract or black cataract
- Headache or sudden loss of eyesight
- Less visible after waking up in the morning

Reasons:
Causes of Diabetic Retinopathy
Diabetes, if left for a long time, it also affects other parts of the body and this affected part can also be eyes. Diabetes affects the blood vessel wall, weakening the vasculature carrying oxygen to the retina (which forms the image). Diabetes patients may suffer from the problem of diabetic retinopathy if the amount of sugar is not controlled. This problem is known when the disease takes serious form.
A major cause of blindness is also 'diabetic retinopathy'. There are two main stages of diabetic retinopathy. The initial stage is called non proliferative diabetic retinopathy (NPDR). In this stage the ducts of the retinal region are damaged. This is usually the initial stage of the disease, in which the symptoms are not detected.
In some cases, blood flows into the central part of the retina due to rupture of damaged blood vessels. This condition is called diabetic maculopathy, which affects vision and causes blurred vision. Its advanced and developed stage is called proliferative diabetic retinopathy (PDR). It is the most severe phase of diabetic retinopathy. In this stage, weak undesirable blood vessels in the retinal area rapidly develop which disrupt the oxygen supply of the retina and damage it. This can also result in retinal detachment or glaucoma. PDR can cause severe vision impairment in about 20 percent of diabetes sufferers, which causes blindness.

Treatments:
Some tips for safety (Tips to prevent diabetic retinopathy)
Periodically check the eyes, this test is also necessary in children.
- Control the amount of cholesterol and sugar in the blood.
If you see symptoms like eye pain, dark sores, see a doctor immediately.
- Diabetes patients should have their eyes checked at least once a year.
- After ten years of diabetes, check the eyes every three months.
- If the pregnant woman is diabetic then contact the doctor.
Treatment for diabetic retinopathy
- Eat more vitamin A rich foods
- Include Spinach in Your Food
- Drink the juice of black grape seeds
- Eat more of salad


Disease: Glaucoma

Description:
Glaucoma
Glaucoma, black cataract or glaucoma disease, causes severe and continuous damage to the system and gradually reduces vision. Rays of light from an object reach the eyes, and its image is formed on the retina. This information from the retina is transmitted to the brain by electrical waves through eye fibers. A fluid is filled in the eye, this fluid keeps the eyeball smooth, if the leakage of this fluid stops, then the pressure inside the eye increases. The difference in glaucoma is that the pressure on the eye exceeds the ability of the affected eye to bear pressure, resulting in damage to the optic nerve, causing loss of vision.
When viewing an object, a person with glaucoma only sees the center of the object. The situation gets worse from time to time. Generally people pay very little attention to it, but by the time they pay attention, it is too late. In general, the disease develops without any symptoms and affects both eyes simultaneously. Although the disease is found among adults over the age of 40, it can also affect newborns in some cases. Diabetes, heredity, high blood pressure and heart disease are among the leading causes of this disease. Globally, black cataract affects about 60 million people and is the second most frequent cause of blindness in India.

Symptoms:
- Tubelight or bulb light begins to appear blurred from all around, intense pain also starts in the eyes.
- Blurring, many patients even stop appearing at night
- nausea or vomiting
- Headache

Reasons:
Causes of Glaucoma
The cornea located in the human eye has the correct shape and nourishing fluid (Aqueous Humor Fluid) to the eye, the ciliary tissues around the lens keep this fluid continuously. This fluid is produced by the pupils in the inner part of the eye. In this way, the formation and flow of this fluid in the eyes continues continuously.
It is necessary for healthy eyes, how much pressure in the inner part of the eye depends on the amount of fluid. The pressure of this fluid in the eyes of glaucoma patients is highly increased, sometimes the passage of the eye's drainage ducts is blocked, but the ciliary tissue continues to make it continuously, when the pressure of the fluid over the optic nerve in the eye Suddenly there is glaucoma. If this pressure of liquid remains in the eyes for a long time, then the fibers of the eyes can also be destroyed. If this disease is not treated in time, it can cause complete loss of vision.

Treatments:
Treatment and tips to prevent Glaucoma
- Eat more spinach in food
Vitamin A is very important for eye health. Eat foods that are vitamin A replenished.
- Fennel is also a good home recipe for healthy eyes.

Disease: Eye Infection

Description:
Eye Infection
Infections in the eye are caused by harmful microbial bacteria and viruses. These harmful microorganisms are most active during the monsoon month. They attack the upper part of the eye, pupil, cornea and eyelids, causing swelling, irritation in the eyes. The eye becomes more red than needed and the water starts to discharge more than necessary.

Symptoms:
- watery eyes
- Pus in the eyes
- Blurred Vision
Dry eye
- Swelling on the eyelids

Reasons:
Causes and Reasons of Eye Infection
Eyelid eyelids are most affected by eye infections. Swelling of the inner part of the eyelids only ends the beauty of the eyes, there is a risk of wounding due to not getting timely treatment. When the infection affects the tear gland inside the eye, the tear gland closes due to swelling and it causes a lot of pain. The most serious condition occurs when the infection affects the cornea. There is a risk of corneal ulcers and lasts until the light of the eyes.
Conjunctivitis - Conjunctivitis is the most common eye infection, also called pink eye. It is a viral infection that spreads quite quickly. If the mother has an infection, then the newborn can also have this infection.
Viral keratitis - Like pink eye, it is also a common eye infection caused by the herpes simplex virus. It also spreads quite rapidly.
Fungal keratitis - This is a fungal infection that can occur by applying a contact lens to the eye. In 2006, this infection came into the limelight when many people fell prey to the use of a particular contact lens solution. However, fungal infection in the eyes is caused by any type of injury or by the passing of organic matter.
Trachoma - This infection is very serious and spreads rapidly in dirty places. This infection occurs when flies and insects thrive on dirt. Trachoma infects the eyelid under the eye, if it persists for a long period of time, there is a risk of wounding in the cornea, which can make the patient blind forever.
Endophthalmitis - When the infection of the eye affects deep enough inside the eye, it is called endophthalmitis. It is caused by both viral and bacterial infections. There is a risk of deep eye injury.

Disease: Jaundice

Description:
Jaundice
Jaundice is a disease caused by a particular type of virus and due to an increase in the amount of bile i.e. Bilirubin Disorder in the body due to some reason. In this, the patient has yellow urine. The white part of his nails, skin and eyes turn yellow and the patient starts complaining of weakness, constipation, nausea, headache, loss of appetite etc.
It is caused by very subtle virus (Virus). Initially, when the disease is slow and mild, then its symptoms are not visible, but when it becomes severe, the eyes and nails of the patient begin to appear yellow. Depending on the virus with which it occurs, there are mainly three types of jaundice (Types of Jaundice), viral hepatitis A, viral hepatitis B and viral hepatitis non A and non B. Jaundice also occurs due to increased acidity in the body, malaria for a long time, stones stuck in the bile duct, drinking too much alcohol, consuming too much salt and sharp substances and lack of blood vessels in the blood.

Symptoms:
- Yellowing of the white part of the eye
- Gastric swelling
- Nausea
- Skin yellowing
- Heavyness and pain under the right ribs
- The color of feces due to bile becomes faded or white
- Stomach ache
- Not feeling hungry
- Continuous weight loss
- Feeling tired in the evening and having fever around 102 degree

Reasons:
Causes and Reasons of Jaundice
When red blood cells in the body break down in a 120-day cycle under a natural process, bilirubin (Bilirubin Disorder) is produced as a waste by-product. Through bilirubin, all the body's dirt is filtered out of the liver and comes out. This dirt comes out through urine and feces. If there is a liver infection or if the amount of bilirubin in the blood exceeds 2.5, then the process of cleaning the dirt of the liver is blocked and jaundice occurs in this condition.
Other Reasons & Causes of Jaundice
If an infection causes the red blood cell to break down before its normal process, then the amount of bilirubin in the blood starts increasing. This situation is called pre hepatic jaundice. The amount of bilirubin in the blood suddenly increases due to malaria, skill cell anemia, thalissemia and also due to many genetic reasons, which causes jaundice (Piliya) disease.
If the liver is damaged due to any reason, then the ability of the liver to produce bilirubin is reduced. It is also called intra-hepatic jaundice. Viral hepatitis, alcoholism of the liver, high fever (liver), liver cancer, incorrect drug intake and excessive intake of paracetamol (medicine side effects) also cause intra-hepatic jaundice. . Obesity carries the risk of liver cirrhosis. This leads to the possibility of intra-hepatic jaundice.
Stones in gall bladder, pancreas not functioning properly, pancreas cancer or gall bladder cancer also stop the process of removing the liver by-product bilirubin from the body. The result is a significant increase in the amount of bilirubin in the blood and severe jaundice occurs.

Treatments:
Care and Treatment for Jaundice
- IV fluids in case of dehydration when dehydration occurs.
- Antibiotics
- Antiviral medicines
- Blood transfusions
- steroids
- Chemotherapy, radiation therapy and phototherapy for the newborn (chemotherapy / radiation therapy & phototherapy for newborns)
Boil milk and water and drink.
- Eat fresh and clean and warm food.
- Use clean toilet only.
- Let syringes be boiled for 20 minutes.
Always use clean and bacteria free water for drinking.
- The hands should be washed thoroughly with soap after cooking, serving, before and after eating and after defecation.
- The food should be covered with a forged cupboard or cover so that it can be protected from flies and dust.
- Do not let the children go to school or outside the doctor until they are told that the disease is free.
- Take blood only after thoroughly examining the blood donors. If the amount of bilirubin in the blood is high then you can also have jaundice.

Disease: Hyper Myopia

Description:
Hyper myopia
In foresight or vision defects, one can easily and clearly see distant things while the nearest objects appear blurr. Vision impairment is called hyperopia in health parlance. How serious the vision defect is depends on your ability to see.
Two parts of the eye are responsible for viewing, the cornea and the lens. The cornea is the transparent part of the front of the eye, while the lens is made inside the eye, which changes the shape of things when they are seen. The cornea and the lens both work together and mix the incoming light and focus it on the retina. The retina is behind the eye ball. When light enters the eye, it is unable to focus properly, that is the vision of the vision. Even if the eyeball is smaller than normal, far-sightedness can occur. Farsightedness is a very common problem that can be easily corrected.

Symptoms:
- Abnormal fatigue feeling.
- Burning or pain around the eye
- to be stressed
- Blurred vision (close to the eye)
- Difficulty reading and writing

Reasons:
Causes & Reasons of Hyper Myopia
In farsightedness or foresight defects, distant things appear clean and nearby things are blurred. In the state of eye rest, parallel rays of light are focussed somewhat behind the sensitive layer of the retina. This is why a person has trouble seeing things nearby. Apart from this, if the parents have far-sightedness then it can also affect the children. Apart from this, this problem can also start with aging. The easiest way to overcome farsightedness is through eyeglasses or contact lenses. By using lenses, we are able to focus better on the light entering the eyes.

Treatments:
Treatment and Tips to Prevent Hyper Myopia
- Should not read lately.
- There should be better illumination during reading and writing.
- Green vegetables and fruits must be used in food.
- Do not work continuously on TV or computer, do not watch continuously.
- When working on TV or computer, it is necessary to have sufficient light in the room.

Disease: Ulcer

Description:
Ulcer
Ulcers in the stomach or small intestines are known as peptic ulcers. Peptic ulcers of the stomach are also called gastric ulcers. Ulcers are caused by diet and stress or by the accumulation of excess acid in the stomach. Gastric ulcer is a more common disease than stomach ulcer. Peptic ulcer is caused by a hole in the thin safety wall between the stomach and stomach after a wound. Long-term antibiotics, pain, and steroid medication, apart from alcohol consumption, cause stomach and stomach ulcers. The formation of acid and enzymes in the stomach leads to a hole or wound near the stomach above the small intestine which is called ulcer.
Mostly it is caused by infection with a bacterium named Helicobacter pylori. In some people, the symptoms of ulcers are easy, while in others they do not appear quickly. Sometimes the ulcer also occurs to those who have not experienced any of its symptoms.

Symptoms:
- If stomach pain is due to ulcers, then at night and whenever you are hungry, it can suddenly become intense.
- Feeling hungry after two hours of eating.
- Increase in gas and belching.
- Feeling tired.
- Feeling full, and inability to drink a lot of fluids.
- loss of appetite.
- Weight loss.
- Pain at any place between the bones of the chest and the navel of the stomach.
- Mild nausea, which is most common when waking up in the morning.

Reasons:
Causes of Ulcers
There is no one specific cause that is responsible for ulcers. Ulcers are caused by the effects of many causes. But it is clear that due to the imbalance of Bach enzyme and digestive juices of stomach and stomach, ulcer is formed from the acid which is formed.
Most ulcers are usually caused by infection with H. Pylori bacteria. This bacterium remains the security wall between the stomach and small intestine. Usually it causes no harm. But due to its infection, sometimes the inner surface of the stomach and the intestines become inflamed, which later takes the form of ulcer.
Frequent intake of pen killers and anti-inflammatory drugs leads to inflammation and piercing of the safety wall between the small intestine and the stomach, causing ulcers.
There are many reasons (Other Reason for Ulcer)
Excess consumption of alcohol and smoking
Due to some serious illness
Due to radiation therapy
Who can have Ulcer (Whom May be More Prone to Ulcer)
People who have a higher risk of developing it, despite having a lot of causes of stomach ulcers, are:
People infected with H. pylori bacteria.
People who regularly take drugs or drugs with needles.
People with a family history of ulcers.
People who drink regularly.
People with liver, kidney, or lung diseases.
People over 50 years old.

Treatments:
Treatment for Ulcer

Disease: Cerebral Stroke

Description:
The continuous supply of oxygen and nutrients to the brain and nerves in our body is done by blood from blood vessels. Whenever there is any damage or formation of obstruction in these blood vessels, the blood supply to some parts of the brain is stopped. Just as heart failure occurs due to lack of blood supply to the heart, similarly some part of the brain is destroyed due to lack of life and nutrients for more than 3 to 4 minutes of blood, it also causes brain attack. it is said.

Symptoms:
- Weakness in Body
- Trouble in understanding directions and directions
- Headache
- Confusion
- Trouble speaking
- Nausea and vomiting
- Numbness in the face, hands or legs on one side of the body
- Slow or unclear
- Sudden faltering, dizziness, deteriorating body balance
- Difficulty seeing with one or both eyes

Reasons:
Causes of brain attack (Causes & Reasons of Cerebral Stroke)
There are mainly 2 reasons for brain attack, which are:
1. Ischemic stroke - The most common cause of seizures. It is caused by the narrowing of a blood vessel or formation of obstruction in the brain. It is also of two types -
1.1. Thrombotic stroke - This type of brain attack causes blockage of blood in the brain's blood vessel or due to clotting. In patients who have a high level of evidence of cholesterol inside the blood, fat is stored in the blood vessels of such patients, which is called plaque. When the blood clot accumulates on it, gradually the entire blood vessel gets blocked and thrombotic stroke occurs when the part of the brain does not get blood.
1.2. Embolic stroke - In this type of brain attack, a small bubble of air entered into the blood vessel accidentally enters the blood vessel by a blood clot or injection or saline causes a small block of blood to build up in the blood vessel. And if there is no blood in that part of the brain, there is an embolic stroke.
2. Hemorrhagic stroke - This type of brain attack due to bleeding in any blood vessel of the brain is very serious. Hypertension, congenital malformation of the blood vessel, or blood vessel inflammation may cause brain haemorrhage. There are two types of it-
2.1. Intra-cranial hemorrhage - In this type of brain hemorrhage due to lack of blood supply to that part of the brain due to bleeding in a blood vessel of the brain. High blood pressure is the leading cause of this type of brain attack. The blood vessel becomes weak and stiff due to high blood pressure continuously for a long time and consequently ruptures.
2.2. Sub-archnoid hemorrhage - In this type, blood accumulates in the sub archnoid space due to bleeding in a blood vessel in the level between the brain and cranium. The main cause of this is congenital malformation of the blood vessel or inflammation in the blood vessel. In this type, the patient experiences a severe headache.
2.3. Transient ischemic attack - There is also a third type of temporary brain attack in which the symptoms of stroke last for a few minutes to a few hours and are cured later. This is called a transient ischemic attack or TIA. It warns that you have a problem and you may have a stroke in the near future if you do not get it treated.

Treatments:
Remedies to avoid brain attack (Treatments & Tips to Prevents Cerebral Stroke)
- Stop alcohol and smoking.
- Fruits, vegetables etc. diet should be taken.
- Stay away from stress. Do regular exercise and yoga.
- If you are overweight then keep your weight under control.
- If there is a problem of repeated headaches, get it checked by a doctor.
- If you are suffering from Hypertension, Diabetes, Heart disease, then get regular medical check up.

In such a situation, the picture of anything, rather than being built on the retina, is made in front of it, which makes things appear blurred. This problem increases with age. People struggling with the problem of myopia can get rid of the problem through glasses or contact lenses, but if the problem is more, then the treatment of myopia by operation is possible.

Description:
The sound and vibrations that come with breath at bedtime is called snoring. Snoring is a simple problem, but when it takes the form of illness, it becomes a serious problem. Heart attack can also occur when this problem increases.

Symptoms:
- Dry throat and nose when waking up in the morning
- Feeling sleepy during the day

Causes & Reasons of Snoring
Most people think that the reason for snoring is excessive fatigue, so they ignore it. This makes the problem serious. Actually, obstruction of breath while sleeping is the main reason for snoring. When the back of the throat becomes narrower, the oxygen passes through the narrow space, causing the surrounding tissue to vibrate. Snoring comes from this only.
Many times people fall asleep on their back, causing the tongue to fall backwards. The back of the palate starts moving to the uvayal (a little meat hanging behind the palate), which prevents breathing and exhaling. This causes the breath to sound and vibrate. Shortening of the lower jaw is also a reason for snoring. When a person's jaw is smaller than normal, when lying down, his tongue turns backwards and blocks the windpipe. In such a situation, pressure has to be applied to breathe and leave, due to which vibration occurs. Crooked Nose Bone and meat soar. In this too, pressure has to be applied to breathe.

- Sleep on the side of your back instead of sleeping. This does not obstruct the windpipe. Sleeping with the head slightly elevated at bedtime. This will not obstruct your tongue and windpipe.
- If the reason for snoring is excess weight, then control weight in time. Join the gym. Weight can be controlled by doing regular yoga and exercise.

Melanin is a pigment that is responsible for the color of the skin. The skin of dark or dark people is less damaged than that of white people because pigment is more formed in dark skin. Pigments are less in white people, so their skin is quickly damaged when exposed to the sun. Apart from this, the skin of people living in hill areas is also damaged more quickly than people living in the grounded area because the sun is closer and brighter than the ground.

Disease: Mumps

Description:
Mumps
Mumps is a viral infection. Although it can affect many parts of the body, however, it mainly affects the salivary glands that are located behind each cheek between the ear and jaw. Mumps cause inflammation of the salivary glands and pain. This disease is mainly seen in the age of 5 to 15 years. This disease occurs sooner in girls than boys (Specially in girl).
Treatment of mumps with antibiotics is not possible, it ends on its own in two weeks. Pain relievers such as ibuprofen or paracetamol can be used, and applying cold packs to the swollen area also helps. A simple examination can confirm mumps because swelling of the jaw is seen just in front of the ears. The diagnosis can also be confirmed by culture or blood test. The presence of antibodies in the blood easily confirms viral infection.

Symptoms:
- Ear ache
- Stomach ache
- Loss of appetite
- Chewing and swallowing pain
- fever
- Headache
- Swelling of cheeks
- Weakness

Reasons:
Reasons & Causes of Mumps
Mumps or mumps is a disease caused by viral infections in the parotid glands. These glands make saliva which is located below the jaw bone on either side of the face. It spreads from one person to another by infecting saliva, sneezing or coughing and sharing utensils with the infected person.
A patient infected with the mumps virus can spread the infection up to 7 days before and 7 days after inflammation begins in the parotid gland. Symptoms usually begin 14–18 days after exposure to the virus. It is said that a person suffers from mumps only once, but some people can become infected again. Sharing of mumps, food and water can also spread. Although this disease is more common in children, but its symptoms can affect a person of any age. It is not a very serious disease but sometimes the problem also increases.

Disease: Prostate Disorder

Description:
Prostate Disorder
When the prostate gland is enlarged, it is called Prostate Disorder. About thirty percent of men are troubled by prostate problems at the age of 40 and more than fifty percent by age 60. The prostate gland is also considered the second heart of men. The prostate gland performs some very important functions in the body. Such as controlling the flow of urin and creating semen for reproduction. As the age progresses, this gland begins to grow. The growth of this gland itself is harmful and it is called Benign Prostatic Hyperplasia.
Increased enlargement of the prostate gland leads to discomfort of urine excretion. As the size of the gland increases, the urinary tube gets blocked and this causes the urine to stop.

Symptoms:
- Waking up for urination several times in the night.

- Difficulty urinating.

- It feels like urine is coming but when going to the bathroom, there is a drop or drop of urine.
- Burning sensation in urine.
- Pain in the testicles continues.
- Urination soon.
- Delay in running urine.

Treatments:
Treatment & Tips to Prevent Prostate Disorder
The patient requires medical treatment when the prostate gland is enlarged. Continuous filling of the urine sac increases the pressure on the kidneys, causing the risk of their malfunctioning. In the early stages of the disease, drugs are tried to reduce the growth of the gland. Some patients have no benefit from medicines, in which case the prostate gland is removed from the patient's body after surgery. With the modern method of medicine, it is possible to treat prostate gland disease by at least incision and bleeding. One such modern technique is prostatectomy with laser rays.
Laser Prostatectomy
In this, part of the prostate gland is cut apart by laser rays, which was blocking the passage of the urinary tube. In laser prostatectomy a fiber optic telescope telescope is sent from the patient's ureter to the bladder. Here the enlarged portion of the prostate gland is removed and the piece of prostate is pushed into the bladder. A tube is inserted into the urethra, which causes urine to flow uninterruptedly. The remaining parts of the gland pushed into the bladder are removed from there.
The pieces of the prostate are sent for pathology examination where the reasons for increasing the size of the gland are investigated. After removal of the prostate gland from laser surgery, complaints like increased frequency of urination, intense desire and complete bladder emptying, and urine flow also recover.
What problem can be removed by removing the prostate gland? (Problems to Remove Prostate Gland)
The secretion of the prostate gland nourishes and protects the sperm. The removal of the gland by surgery has no adverse effect because in addition to the prostate, seminal vesicles also perform this function.

Description:

Let's know full information about Zika virus and its infection (Zika Virus Information in Hindi).

Symptoms:
- Reddening of eyes
- Joint pain
- fever
- vomiting
- Weakness

Treatments:
Treatment of Zika Virus
* According to the CDC, no injection or medicine has yet been invented to fight zika infection. A person suffering from this should take complete rest, drink plenty of water, take normal fever medicines.
* You should protect yourself from mosquito bites if infected with zika virus, otherwise this virus can reach others by mosquitoes. It is very important to protect the suffering patient from mosquitoes.
Note: In case of fever, medicines like aspirin, Brufen should not be taken at all.
Tips for Pregnant Women
The CDC has suggested pregnant women living in other countries not to go to Africa, South America or other countries affected by zika. Pregnant women living in areas affected by zika virus should take care of the following:
* You should protect yourself from mosquito bites.
* Mosquito nets should be used while sleeping at night and cream that protects against mosquito bites.
* If symptoms like headache, light fever, red eyes, joint pain are seen on mosquito bite, a doctor should be consulted immediately.
* Pregnancy plan should be postponed for a few days if not pregnant.
Pregnant women should try their best to avoid mosquitoes because the zika virus causes the most damage to the brains of babies in their womb.

- Skin pain is experienced
- Conjunctivitis
- Pimples all over the body
- The palate of the mouth turns red
- Mouth, ear, nose bleeding
- These symptoms are also seen in the advanced stage of the disease.

Reasons:

Treatments:
There is no concrete treatment for Ebola yet. Avoidance is considered the best remedy for this disease. Till now the following steps are taken in the case of victims of Ebola:
- There is no specific treatment for this disease; Efforts to help infected people include oral rehydration therapy (giving them a little sweet and salty water to drink) or intravenous fluids.
- Often 50% to 90% of the people infected with this virus are killed.
- Efforts are on to develop vaccines for this; However, no such vaccine exists yet.

7. Sweat and Dust- When the sweat that comes on the skin of the head comes in contact with dust during summer, dirt starts to accumulate on the scalp. Which slowly causes dandruff.
8. Allergies- Many times the oil, shampoo, hair styling product or hair color we are using does not suit us, the result is an allergy which is a big reason for dandruff.

Description:

One should stay away from infected people to avoid this.

Symptoms:
- H1N1 patients feel very tired.
- In H1N1, the sufferer feels a lot of intensity of muscle pain, stiffness and pains.

- In about 80% of H1N1 cases, the patient heats with fever. In fever, the body temperature reaches 101 degrees. Fever increases continuously even after taking the medicine.
- Constant head pain is a common symptom of H1N1 and is present in 80% of patients.

Reasons:
Swine flu is believed to spread rapidly among people living close to most pigs. Though there are many other factors which are responsible for swine flu but the most important reason of these is the contact of pigs. Some other factors are:
Causes of Swine Flu
- Individuals living with infected pigs may come in the grip of swine flu and later they can infect others.
- The risk of disease is more in children, elderly, pregnant women and people with heart, kidney, diabetes. Those who have low immunity can also become victims of swine flu.
It is important to note here that properly cooked red meat does not cause swine flu but if care is taken carelessly, there can be some problems.

Treatments:
The best way to avoid swine is to avoid it. This disease can be easily avoided by staying away from the infected patient. Some other measures are:
Staying away from infected people is the prevention of this disease.

- Avoid touching eyes, nose or mouth with dirty hands and avoid eating outside.
- Avoid close contact with sick people
- Wear a mask before going to the hospital or any other public place.
If necessary, go to an infected person and wear a mask as well as gloves. With this you can stay safe from disease.
Swine flu vaccine is present in India to avoid swine flu. Swine flu vaccine protects you from this disease for one year.
- On seeing the symptoms of swine flu, the patient should be hospitalized immediately so that he can be treated properly.
If you are suffering from influenza, then you should stay away from other people to protect them from infection.

Disease: Dehydration

Description:
Dehydration means dehydration. The state of depletion of water in human body is called dehydration. In scientific language, dehydration is called Hypohydration. Due to lack of water in the body (Pani ki Kami), mineral substances such as salt and sugar are reduced from the body. During dehydration, water from the body's cells keeps drying up, causing the body's balance of functioning to become abnormal.

Symptoms:
- Nervousness or shivering
- Constipation
- dizziness
- Mouth Drying
- Dry skin
- Not quenching thirst
- Headache
Sloth
- muscle cramps
- Weakness

Reasons:
- Severe water problem in the body can be fatal at times.
- After exhausting five percent fluid from the body, weakness, thirst, nausea, irritability occur.
- Ten percent fluid from the body is exhausted, headache, dizziness and limb sensation may occur. The skin of the body starts to turn blue and the body becomes weak.
- Fifteen percent fluid from the body is affected by the sight and hearing. The tongue gets swollen and there is difficulty in swallowing food.
- If more than fifteen percent of the fluid is exhausted from the body, a person can also die.
- Due to diarrhea, dehydration in the body increases the chances of death of a human being. Due to severe dehydration (Pani ki Kami), the brain damage of a person can also cause harm to his brain. There is also the risk of hypovolemic shock in which many parts of the body can be harmed.
- If you are dizzy, or you are unable to do any work, then it is very important to see a doctor at such a time. If you have constipation or fever for more than two days, contact the doctor immediately.

Treatments:
Treatment for Dehydration
- Drink as much water as possible.
- For the treatment of dehydration in newborns (pani ki kami ka ilaj), keep giving the baby breast milk and water. Mix ORS solution in water and drink it.
- Do not do too much rushing and relax as much as you can.
- Do not go out of the house in the sun and sit in a cool place.
- Avoid consuming substances like milk, coffee, fruit juice.
- Be sure to consume sports drinks containing electrolytes.

Disease: Prickly Heat

Description:
Prickly heat is called Prickly Heat in English. It is common in the summer season to have rash. During summer season excessive amount of sweat flows from the body. If this sweat is not cleared in time, then it dries in the skin of the body due to which sweat glands are closed and rash starts in the body.

Symptoms:
- Body itching
- Burning sensation or prickling in the body
- Red-pink, small grains appear on the body
- Excessive sweating
- pricking with clothes
- Feeling tired

Reasons:
Itching, mild swelling and stinging are felt in the body during rash. Prickly rash is aggravated by direct exposure to sunlight. Gummour usually goes away on its own in a few days but in some people it can last for weeks and months. Therefore, if the prickly heat does not cure for a week, a doctor should be consulted.
People also complain of heat exhaustion and sunburn due to prickly heat. Prickly heat can also cause danger of heat stroke.
There are also several types of prickly heat, such as Miliaria Crystallina, Miliaria Rubra and Miliaria Profunda. Milaria profunda has the highest risk and is also known as Wildfire Rash.

Treatments:
The best way to prevent heat rash is to stay away from heat. Apart from this, there are some important measures to prevent Ghamoriyan:
- Do not wear clothing made of synthetic fabric.
- Wear cotton and loose-fitting clothes.
- Drink plenty of water and take a shower.
- Take a shower after returning home from outside.
- Allow the body parts to feel fresh.
- Avoid spicy food. Eat plain food only.
- Taking a bath with rain water removes pimples and donations on the body.
- Chew four to five leaves of neem daily in the morning.
- Apply multani mitti on the body.
Boil neem leaves in water and take a bath with this water.
- Mix camphor in coconut oil and massage the whole body with this oil.
- Use calamine lotion.
- Do not apply powder on wet body. Avoid using too much powder.

Symptoms:

Vitamin C deficiency was first seen in traders trading through the sea, who lived outside the house for a long time and could not get proper food. Vitamin C is soluble in water, that is, the body neither makes it nor stores it, so it is necessary to reach the body periodically for better health. Other reasons that can cause scurvy are the following:
- Do not boil cow's milk properly and give it to children.
- If there is not enough of fruits and vegetables in the food, the body cannot get vitamin C.

Disease: Beriberi

Description:
Beriberi is a disease caused by vitamin B1 deficiency. It affects many parts of our body like muscles, heart and digestive power etc. People in those parts of Southeast Asia, where rice is the staple food, suffer in large numbers.

Symptoms:
- Trouble speaking
- Mentally confuse
- Numbness in hands or feet

Reasons:
Reasons of Berberi
Deficiency of vitamin B1 is the main cause of beriberi disease. The disease is less in those who eat plenty of vitamins.
Other Reason (Beriberi)
- Due to alcohol, it is possible that your body is not able to absorb Vitamin B1. Beriberi disease occurs in such a condition. - Doctors believe that due to genetic reasons, there is deficiency of Vitamin B1 in the body.
- Pregnant woman and anyone with hyperthyroidism, ie a person overactive of the thyroid gland, needs additional vitamin B1.
- Some diseases like liver disease do not allow the body to absorb vitamin B1. At such times, there is a risk of beriberi.
Kidney dialysis also increases the risk of getting beriberi disease.

Treatments:
Treatment and Beriberi
Beriberi is treated with thiamine supplementation. In which the doctor undergoes a blood test which shows how well the body is absorbing the vitamins. The doctor will also give you directions on taking certain types of food based on thiamine, in which you will be advised to take cereals, poultry, meat, beets, dry fruits, tomatoes and orange juice etc.
Rice, undercooked and raw meats etc. can become a problem for not absorbing vitamin B1 in your body. To avoid beriberi disease, nutritious and balance diet should be taken which has proper amount of thiamine.
Pregnant and lactating mothers should also be periodically checked for vitamins in the body. Also, such individuals who consume more alcohol should also get vitamin deficiency checked periodically.

Reasons:
Causes of Erectile Dysfunctions
Some people believe that erectile dysfunction is associated with aging, whereas in reality they are not. ED is also caused by hypertension, diabetes and depression etc. Erectile dysfunction can also occur due to physical and mental reasons.
If the erection occurs at any particular time apart from sexual intercourse such as waking up in the morning, while urinating, masturbating or thinking about sex, it can be due to mental reasons.
Keep in mind that stress increases or worsens the levels of many hormones in the body, of which adrenaline and cortisol are the main hormones. Due to these, many unwanted changes occur in the body and the functioning of the nervous system deteriorates, due to which the immune system begins to weaken.
Although ED is related to mental state in only 10 percent of cases, in most cases it is due to hormonal causes or diseases like diabetes and blood pressure.
Physical Causes of Erectile Dysfunctions
According to doctors, in almost 90 percent of cases of erectile dysfunction, the causes are physical, in the remaining 10 percent of cases it is mental. There are several other reasons for this:
* Alcohol, smoking, sugar and stress are its major causes.
* Anomaly in hormones is a major cause of erectile dysfunction.
* When the penis is hard, blood flows in it. Whenever there is a decrease in blood flow in the penis, it is not able to harden properly and problems like erectile dysfunction start.
* Problems related to neurology (any deficiency in the nervous system) can also be the cause of erectile dysfunction.

Treatments:

Hormones Therapy
If the cause of erectile dysfunction is the deficiency or disturbance of the hormone, then it is corrected within two to 2 to 3 months with the help of hormone therapy. This treatment does not have any specific side effects.
Blood supply
If there is a decrease in blood flow due to any kind of blockage in the arteries of the penis, then this blockage is eliminated with the help of drugs. This increases the blood flow to the penis and properly stresses it.

Erectile dysfunction can also be overcome with the help of treatment mediums such as vacuum pumps, injection therapies and Viagra. However some doctors believe that vacuum pumps and injection therapy are now old-fashioned things.
Sex Therapy
As we have mentioned that in some cases of ED, the problem is mental rather than physical. In such cases, with the help of sex therapy, the patient is given detailed information about sex, so that he can avoid this problem by improving his daily and married life.
Blood pressure and heart problems
The main reason for penis hardening is the proper flow of blood in it. But whenever there is a decrease in blood flow in the penis, it is not completely hardened and the problem of erectile dysfunction starts. It is more when there is blood pressure or heart problems, so these problems should be avoided.
Avoid Stress
Stress also causes erectile dysfunction. So stay stress free to avoid erectile dysfunction. Do yoga, meditation and exercise and improve your diet.

Disease: Pellagra

Description:
Pilagra is a disease caused by vitamin B3 deficiency. It is caused by a lack of niacin or tryptophan in the body or an excess of leucine. This disease also degrades the body's protein metabolism, causing many diseases such as Carcinoid Syndrome.

Symptoms:
- Hair fall: We usually have 20 to 50 hair falls every day. Headache also causes hair loss, if it causes more hair loss then it can also be a reason
- Red rashes appear in the body
- Insomnia
- Mentally confuse
- Nerve damage
- Be susceptible to sunlight
- Bloating - Sore mouth
- Weakness

Reasons:
There are several reasons for having Pilagra, some of which are:
Causes of Pellagra
Niacin is responsible for vitamin B3 deficiency, resulting in increased NAD production in most pathologies.
* Another reason is the lack of essential amino acids ie Tryptophan, which is found in abundance in meats, fish, eggs and peanuts. Our body itself converts it into niacin.
* The third reason is the excess of leucine in the body that converts quinolinate phosphoribosyl transferase (Quinolinate Phosphoribosyl Transferase i.e. QPRT) and niacin into nicotinamide mononucleotide.
Medicine Causing Peelagra
Many medicines also cause Pellagra, including antibiotics. In addition, it is also possible that the body is not able to absorb niacin in the body due to any reason. In such a situation, it is better to consult a doctor in this regard and follow the guidelines given by the doctor.
Other factors of Pilagra
If the treatment of Pilagra is not done on time, then the patient can also die in 4 to 5 years. There are many factors that can increase the risk of Pilagra, such as:
* Drinking too much alcohol
* Suffering from a disease called Anorexia Nervosa
* Digestive disease
* Taking small amounts of Tryptophan in food

Treatments:
According to doctors, Pilagra can be avoided even if normal food is taken care of. The following things can be taken care of to reduce the risk of Pilagra:
Treatment of Pellagra
* Pilagra can be avoided by increasing the amount of niacin in food ie Vitamin B3.
* Red meat, fish, poultry, fortified bread, lentils and peanuts, etc., are rich in niacin.
* See your doctor immediately if you eat a low amount of vitamin B3 or your body is unable to absorb niacin due to some disease. For this you can also take niacin supplement or multivitamin or mineral supplement.
These supplements should contain at least 20 mg of niacin. Likewise, a man needs 16 milligrams a day and a woman needs 14 milligrams of niacin.
* Tryptophan-rich food plays a big role in the formation of niacin. For this, you can eat seafood, meats, poultry, green leafy vegetables etc. Apart from this, pulses, fish, milk and yeast can also be included in your diet.
* Do not use alcohol and make a healthy diet plan.

Disease: Rickets

Description:
Rickets is caused by lack of vitamin D. It is a disease in children in which the bones of children become soft. Sometimes the bones become so weak that they are broken even under normal pressure. For this reason, the legs of the children become twisted and the spine turns abnormal. This type of disease is called osteomalacia in the elderly.

Symptoms:
- pain in bones

Reasons:
Deficiency of Vitamin D is a major cause of Rickets disease. Vitamin D is necessary to aid in the exploitation of calcium and phosphorus from the alimentary canal. Calcium and phosphorus are also needed for strengthening the bones of children, so when there is a lack of calcium and phosphorus in the blood of the body, the blood is replenished by the bones and it balances. As a result, the bones become soft and the bone structure becomes weak.
Causes of Rickets
Sun light: Sun light is the main source of vitamin D. But in today's environment, children do not like to play outside the house. Parents also like to engage the child in indoor activity. In such a situation, children do not get enough vitamin D from sunlight.
Food - Children also have to face vitamin D deficiency due to lack of nutritious food. Fish oil, egg yolk and milk etc. also contain sufficient amount of Vitamin D. If these things are not included in the diet plan of the child, then he may be at risk of Rickets.

Treatments:
Due to Rickets, not only physical weakness occurs, but sometimes due to this disease, disability is also seen in children. Following are some easy remedies to avoid this disease:
Remedies for Rickets
* Provide adequate amounts of vitamin D to children.
* It is also necessary to stay in the sun for a while, so give the children a sun bath.
* Pay special attention to eating and drinking. Vitamin supplements can be taken along with plenty of egg yolk, fish and milk.
* Also consult a doctor. Physicians see the negativity of the child by pressing their bones.
* The condition of rickets can also be known by X-rays. Also, by examining urine and blood, the disease and improvement in it can be detected.

Disease: Obesity

Description:
Obesity is an abnormally stored fat inside the body. In general, if the body weight is more in proportion to the length of the person, then it is considered as Motapa but obese people have more fat on their body than the obese people, which not only makes the body unformed but in many ways Also causes other physical problems.

Reasons:
There are many reasons which are directly or indirectly the reasons for obese. A person may become obese due to behavior or lifestyle, the surrounding environment and many genetic reasons.
Causes of Obesity
Lifestyle
In today's fast pace, people easily adopt unhealthy lifestyles. Neither are able to pay attention to food and nor has any physical effort left, in such a situation, obesity easily engulfs people.
Fast food has increased in the food of people, which is mostly made of refined oils and all kinds of refinery oils, in this way people consume more calories but in contrast the physical effort is not reduced due to which the body fat also starts accumulating. And the person becomes obese.
Environment
The environment or surrounding environment also has a great impact on the health of the body. As of now, climbing stairs, descending, walking etc. is no more. Now people want to cover even the shortest distance by car and bike. Also use the lift to climb a floor.
Apart from this, the tradition of eating fresh food is also getting reduced. Canned food or food stored in the fridge, eating habits also do not have a good effect on the body.
Genetic Reason
Science says that some genetic factors are also the cause of obesity. Many types of disorder in jeans also lead to obesity. Also, if the parents are obese, then it is possible that the children are obese. In such a situation, vigilance should be exercised from the beginning.
Eating and Drinking Habit
Your eating and drinking habits can also make your body fat. Eating too much or not eating at once, both conditions are not good for the body. Many people do not eat breakfast in the morning to avoid obesity, while doing so increases obesity.

Treatments:
Some people do not have any time to eat. Untimely eating and drinking habits also increase obesity. Instead of eating on time and eating together, eating in small portions is often better for the body.

Disease: Allergy

Description:
Allergy
Being susceptible to anything is allergy, which in health parlance is also called atopy. Allergies can be from anyone, from changes in weather, from food, from pets, from dust, from smoke, from cosmetics or from drugs.
In allergy, the body's immune system is unable to accept certain things. Immunity responds inappropriately to these things. Allergy is the reaction given by immunity. Like this, most allergies are not dangerous, but sometimes the problem becomes serious.
Allergies can be prevented, but for this the reasons that cause allergies have to be completely avoided. Although allergy is not an infectious disease, even if someone has a runny nose and eye water allergy, it is better to keep in touch with them. If possible, do not use the goods used by him.

Symptoms:
- Eye itching and red eye
- watery eyes
- Eczema and summer fever
- Itchy throat
- Skin itching
- Bile formation on the skin
- Skin rash and rash
- Frequent rash inside the nose
- Repeated nose itching
- Runny nose

Reasons:
Cause of allergy
1. Dust
Dust particles are very small organisms that live on most things around us. These particles grow in high humidity which get their food from dead skin, bacteria and fungus etc.
2. Insect
People who are allergic to pests, the skin becomes red and swollen due to the sting of insect bites. Not only this, they may also have vomiting, dizziness and fever.
3. Food
Some people are also allergic to everyday things such as peanuts, milk and eggs. People with food allergies may experience nausea, body itching, or rash after eating.
4. Rubber (Latex)
Any product made of rubber can cause allergies. Rubber products also harm some people, such as the use of gloves, condoms, medical equipment, etc. can cause irritation, runny nose, sneezing, breathlessness, and itching problems.
5. Fragrance
Smells good but may also cause allergies of some people. The fragrance of perfumes, scented candles, various beauty products, etc. can cause headaches, nausea and nose allergies.
6. Animals
Pets are also the cause of allergies of many people. The hair of animals, saliva coming out of their mouth, dandruff etc. can cause many serious problems.
7. Grass
Sometimes grass, trees and flowers are also the cause of allergies. All these are the cause of seasonal allergies, which can cause itching, eye irritation, frequent sneezing and itching.

Treatments:
Tips to get rid of allergies (Tips to Prevent Allergy)
- Avoid dust, smoke and dirt.
- Be careful in the consumption of some medicines like aspirin, nemusalide etc.
- Reduce the use of sour things like pickles etc.
- Do not eat foods that are allergic to food.
- People with dirt allergy should change the sheets, pillow covers and curtains from time to time.

Disease: Cataract (Cataract)

Description:
Cataract
Cataract is a white colored spot embossed in the eye lens, which affects the vision of the eye. Cataract causes a person to see anything blurred. Cataracts mostly occur in the elderly. Cataract can occur only in one eye or both eyes, even it can spread from one eye to another.

Symptoms:
- White layer deposition on eye lens
- Two things visible with one eye
- Many times even light appears to be very bright
- Light color of any object
- Any object appearing blurred
- Change the number of glasses frequently
- Having trouble with strong light
- Appearance of rings in night light
- Difficulty driving at night
- Eyesight becomes weaker as it is evening

Reasons:
The lens inside the eye acts like a camera. This focuses the light on the retina, making things visible. Lenses consist of water and protein. The protein remains attached to the lens in such a way that it keeps the lens clean so that the light can pass through.
With aging, some proteins accumulate in one place and accumulate on one part of the lens. In this case, cataract occurs due to the formation of excessive protein in the eye lens, which makes the lens blurred. This does not allow the light to go through the lens completely, so that the eye is not clearly visible. In this case, all new lens cells accumulate on the outside of the lens, while all the old lens cells accumulate in the middle of the lens, which is called cataract or cataract.
Other reason & causes of cataract
- Any other disease in the eyes, such as glaucoma etc.
- Congenital eye cataract
- Having diabetes
- Taking steroid for any body trouble, such as asthma
- Sudden exposure to strong light or continuous high light
- Excessive smoking or alcohol consumption

Treatments:
Tips to prevent cataract
- Protect yourself from sunlight or strong light, wear glasses on your eyes and a hat on your head.
- Do not take any kind of intoxication
- eat nutritious food
- Periodically get the eyes checked
- Stay away from stress
- Keep diabetes under control

Home Remedies:
When it comes to the eyes, the problem should be taken seriously, because once the light of the eyes has gone, it cannot be found again. Cataract is also a serious problem, in which a spot on the eye lens comes on the eye lens. Everything that you see makes you look blurred and there you look like a blot.
While cataracts can be removed by surgery, cataracts are also possible with the help of some home remedies. If you are conscious in the beginning, then it is possible that you do not have to undergo surgery or operation.

Eating spinach cures cataracts to a great extent. Spinach has beta carotene and antioxidant properties. By eating spinach daily, the cataract of the eyes ends in a few days and the eyes become as before.

People with cataracts have mostly red eyes and are more difficult to deal with. In such a situation, milk and almonds give benefit to the eyes. Soak almonds in milk overnight for treatment. Sieve this milk in the morning and pour its drops into the eyes and chew the almonds and eat it.

Green tea can cause eye light. Green tea is also beneficial in common eye problems. Drinking green tea three to four times a day is a health benefit to the eyes. Antioxidants present in green tea give freshness to the eyes.

Raw papaya contains an enzyme named Papain which helps in digestion of protein (Protien). People suffering from cataract have difficulty digesting protein, so raw papaya gives benefit to people suffering from cataract. By using raw papaya daily, the lens of the eye starts shining like new.

Disease: Tetanus

Description:
Tetanus
Infection in human wounds causes tetanus, which is due to Clostridium tetani Bacteria. This bacterium produces a toxin in a wound or injury that causes tetanus. Gradually, this poison starts spreading throughout the body, which makes the situation fatal. Many times a person can also die due to tetanus. In tetanus, the muscles of the body feel cramps and stop and hurts. However, if a tetanus vaccine is administered immediately after an injury, then it can be avoided.

Symptoms:
- high blood pressure
- Neck spasms
- Irritability
- Facial muscles
Jaw closure
- Difficulty swallowing
- Sweating profusely
- Muscle cramps and stiffness
- Shortness of breath
- Fast heart rate

Reasons:
Cause of tetanus
Clostridium tetani is a rod-shaped bacterium found in soil around the world. Clostridium titani is the bacterium responsible for tetanus disease. This bacterium is found in two forms, first in dormant or inactive form and second in active form which further increases the number of bacteria. Any type of injury can cause tetanus.
- from wound
- in surgery
- During delivery
- If there is an abscess
- Needle or injection drug users
- Due to injury from an old rusted iron

Treatments:
Tips to avoid tetanus (Tips to Prevent Tetanus)
- Any wound that has ruptured the skin should be cleaned with water and soap immediately.
- Never leave the wound open. The risk of open wound infection is high.
If there is bleeding from the wound, then tie cotton and dry cloth on it.
- To stop the blood, apply pressure on the wound, so that the blood stops flowing.
- The injured person should be vaccinated with tetanus immediately.
Treatment of Tetanus
- Wash the wound with warm water and apply any antiseptic cream or powder.
- Massage the body with turpentine oil, massage it by applying light hand pressure on the feet, jaw and neck.
- Heat oil on the wound and mix turmeric in it.
- Candle wax can also be applied to the wound by melting.
- Applying neem oil to the cut off area also does not fear tetanus.

Sprains

Symptoms:

Disease: low blood pressure or low blood pressure

Description:
Low Blood Pressure
Low blood pressure or low blood pressure prevents oxygen from reaching the brain. Not only oxygen but other nutrients also do not reach the brain. In the language of health, blood pressure is known as hypotension.
Although low blood pressure is not a disease, but it is a sign of other serious disease that is growing in the body. In such a situation, when the blood flow in one's body becomes less than normal, it is called low blood pressure or low blood pressure. Normal blood pressure is 120/80. In such a situation, the heart, kidney, lungs and brain may stop working partially or completely.

Symptoms:
- Darkness in front of eyes
- Vomiting and diarrhea
- Neck stiffness
- dizziness
- Chest pain, shortness of breath
- Cold hands and feet
- Missed beats are felt in the heart

Reasons:
Causes of low blood pressure
1. Heart disease - Decreased blood pressure is associated with severe heart disease, heart disease weakens heart muscle, due to which the heart is unable to pump enough blood and our BP is low. . Heart patients and patients with anemia should be careful about low BP.
2. Arthostatic hypertension type - In this, the patient feels dizzy when standing, as his blood pressure drops by 20 points. It is based on a nervous system. But sometimes the side effects of the medicines can also be caused by allergies.
3. Less blood and other reason - Due to bleeding or lack of blood from internal organs of the body, lack of nutritional or irregularity in food, lung attack, worsening of heart valve. From, low BP may occur. Low BP can also occur from a sudden shock, a horrific scene or hearing the news.
Other reason & causes of low blood pressure
- Pregnancy, hormone imbalances such as decreased activation of thyroid
- With the effect of blood sugar medicines
Stroke and liver diseases
- Some essential vitamins like B12 and iron deficiency

Treatments:
What to do if you have low blood pressure (some tips to prevent low blood pressure)
- Sit or lie down immediately, clench, tie, open, move your feet.
- Drink water or tea with salt and sugar. Lay two pillows under your feet.
- Those who are already eating high BP medicine, stop eating the medicine.
- Drink at least eight glasses of water and other drinks daily.
- Reduce the amount of carbohydrates in the food.
Apart from all these, seek medical advice immediately.

Home Remedies:
- People with low blood pressure should eat more salt
- If you feel dizzy constantly, drink more water
- Drink a cup of sweet potato juice twice a day
- Soak raisins in an earthen pot overnight. Chew raisins in the morning and eat water
- In the morning on an empty stomach, eat honey mixed with basil leaf juice
- Soak almonds in the night, peel off these almond peels in the morning and boil them with milk. Drink this milk lukewarm.

Cause of gray hair
The color of hair is black, white or brown depending on the melanin. Those who lack melanin in their hair have a lighter hair color, those who have more melanin in their hair have black hair. People whose hair turns white have melanin in their hair. Melanin pigments reside in the hair follicle. In some cases, hair may turn white due to thyroid, anemia or genetic reasons.

Disease: Bone fracture or dislocation

Description:
Bone fracture or dislocation
Fracture - Fracture of bone is called bone fracture. Bone can be broken due to many reasons, from falling somewhere, due to collision, jerk or sudden pressure.
Dislocation of bone - When two bones move from a connected place, it is called dislocation or bone shifting. Two bones join on one joint, but due to injury on this joint, the bones are moved from this joint. There is also a lot of pain due to the movement of bones and swelling occurs at the respective place.

Symptoms:
- Unbearable pain
- Stiffness due to damage in nearby nerves
- Inflammation at the site of fracture
- Instability in the tissue surrounding the fracture
- Fracture site completely stopped
- to faint

Reasons:
Causes of bone frtacture or dislocation

- Nerve additions around the bones, which become active upon breaking of the bone, indicate pain to the brain.
- Bleeding and swelling due to breaking of bones, causing pain.
- When fractured, the muscles shrink and try to save the bone, it also causes pain.
- In case of any accident which affects the bones.
- Fracture of bones also depends on the age of the person because the chances of fracture increase with old age.
Unbearable pain may also occur in some situations like-
- Infection
- Wrongly plaster, too loose or too tight

Treatments:
Treatment- (Tips to prevent bone fracture or dislocation)
- Ice the fractured area. The swelling will reduce and the pain will get relief.
- The sufferer should rest completely. If possible, avoid moving the respective place.
- Warm compresses also provide relief.
- If the bone of the hand or leg is broken, keep it at a height.
- Massage the area around the fractured area.
- Eat half a pineapple daily.
- Avoid eating red meat.
- Do not eat preservative food.
Precautions
- Always wear a seat belt while sitting in the car.
- While playing a sport or riding a bicycle and motorcycle, wear the associated safety equipment.
- If someone has osteoporosis, then exercise regularly and take a bone-strengthening diet.

Disease: Chicken Pox - Chickenpox

Description:
Chicken pox - Chickenpox
Smallpox is a viral infection that causes blisters on the body like blisters and itching. Smallpox is more common to people who do not fall ill or who have not been vaccinated to avoid smallpox. In the earlier times, everyone was affected by smallpox once or until young, but in today's time such diseases have decreased. For most people, smallpox is a mild disease. Nevertheless, it is better to be vaccinated. Smallpox vaccines are a safe and effective way to prevent smallpox and its potential complications.

Symptoms:
- Feeling tired (weakness)
- fever, headache
- loss of appetite
- Red-pink, small grains appear on the body

Reasons:
Which people are at greater risk? (Risk Factors of Chicken Pox)
Chickenpox is highly infected, and it can spread rapidly. Others may be exposed to bacteria in the air by coming into direct contact with the rash of the virus or by coughing or sneezing. The risk of smallpox (chechak) is more when:
- Nobody has ever had chicken pox.
- Have not been vaccinated for smallpox.
- Children who have been affected by infection in school or hostels.

Treatments:
Treatments of Chicken Pox
- After dissolving one teaspoon of baking soda in a glass of water, apply this water on the body with the help of cotton. You will get relief from smallpox.
- To avoid itching during smallpox, take oatmeal in water and take a bath.
- To avoid itching from smallpox (calamine lotion), apply calamine lotion over the grains.
- Apply honey to the affected area two to three times a day.
- To cure smallpox quickly, drink carrot and green coriander soup.
- Soak cotton in sandalwood oil and apply it on the affected area.
- Make a paste by boiling green peas, apply it on the grains, it will get relief.
- Remove the fresh juice of aloe vera and apply it on the seeds.
Tips for Chicken Pox
- If you have fever with smallpox, then drink plenty of beverages. Take water, juice and soup from time to time. If the child drinks the milk of the infected mother, the mother should not be fed milk.
- Do not scratch the grains and keep your nails small. Wear gloves on your hands to avoid scratching at bedtime.
- Keep the body cool to avoid itching. Wear light clothes and avoid bathing with hot water.
- Also make sure that the infection does not spread to other members of the household. Keep away the clothes, bedding etc. of the infected person and wash them separately from the clothes of other members of the household.

Home Remedies:
Rapid itching, red rash in the body are the main symptoms of chicken pox. Children between 1 and 10 years of age have a higher risk of chicken pox. Irregularity in food is the main cause of spread of chicken pox. During this time one should not try to remove the rashes from the nail, by doing so it spreads.
At the time of smallpox (Chechak), proper food should be taken care of. Avoid eating spicy and oily food. Aspirin should never be given to a chickenpox patient. This can make his condition worse. Avoid going outside and in crowded areas when chicken pox occurs. If possible, stay away from people during this time.
Know Home Remedies for Chicken pox
The disease can be relieved by adopting the following remedies:
1. Oat Flour - There is very strong itching in the body when chicken pox occurs. To avoid itching, bath with oat flour should be mixed with water. Mix 2 cups of oat flour in 2 liters of water and boil it for about 15 minutes, tie the cooked flour well in a cotton bag and put it in a bath tub and take a bath.
2. Brown Vinegar - Taking half a cup of brown vinegar in water and taking a bath can relieve itching. This reduces the swelling of the grains and also causes the grains to dry up.
3. Lemon Juice - Drinking lemon juice provides relief in chicken pox. For treatment, squeeze lemon in a glass of clean water from time to time.
4. Margosa Leaves - Taking neem leaves in warm water and taking bath, itching ends. Neem is naturally rich in anti-bacterial properties. In this case, chicken pox is very beneficial in healing.
5. Baking Soda - Mix half a teaspoon of baking soda in a glass of lukewarm water and allow this paste to dry on the entire body. This causes chickenpox to heal quickly.
6. Apple Cider Vinegar - Mixing half a cup of apple vinegar in lukewarm water and taking a bath provides relief. Sit in this water for about 20 minutes.
7. Vitamin E Oil - Applying vitamin-E oil on the body relieves itching during chicken pox.
8. Carrot - Eating boiled carrots and coriander reduces the weakness of chicken pox. Drinking a carrot and coriander soup relieves it.
9. Herbal Tea - Make tea by adding basil, marigold and chamomile, then drink honey or lemon mixed with it. Drinking this tea 3-4 times a day gives relief.
10. Green Pea - Cook green peas in water and apply its water in the body, it ends the rash of chicken pox.
